                    window.guardian.mustardCut = false;
                </script>
<script>
                    // Noop monkey patch perf.mark and perf.measure if not supported
                    if(window.performance !== undefined && window.performance.mark === undefined) {
                        window.performance.mark = function(){};
                        window.performance.measure = function(){};
                    }
                </script>
<script>
                    // record the number of times the browser goes offline during a pageview
                    window.guardian.offlineCount = 0;
                    window.addEventListener('offline', function incrementOfflineCount () { window.guardian.offlineCount++ });
                </script>
<script>
                    // this is a global that's called at the bottom of the pf.io response,
                    // once the polyfills have run. This may be useful for debugging.
                    // mainly to support browsers that don't support async=false or defer
                    function guardianPolyfilled() {
                        window.guardian.polyfilled = true;
                        if (window.guardian.mustardCut === false) {
                            window.guardian.queue.forEach(function(callback) { callback() })
                        }
                    }

                    // We've got contracts to abide by with the Ophan tracker
                    // Setting pageViewId here ensures we're not getting race-conditions at all
                    window.guardian.config.ophan = {
                        // This is duplicated from
                        // https://github.com/guardian/ophan/blob/master/tracker-js/assets/coffee/ophan/transmit.coffee
                        // Please do not change this without talking to the Ophan project first.
                        pageViewId:
                            new Date().getTime().toString(36) +
                            'xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/x/g, function() {
                                return Math.floor(Math.random() * 36).toString(36);
                            }),
                    };
                </script>
<script>
                    // Set the browserId from the bwid cookie on the ophan object created above
                    // This will need to be replaced later with an async request to an endpoint
                    (function (window, document) {

                        function getCookieValue(name) {
                            var nameEq = name + "=",
                                cookies = document.cookie.split(';'),
                                value = null;
                            cookies.forEach(function (cookie) {
                                while (cookie.charAt(0) === ' ') {
                                    cookie = cookie.substring(1, cookie.length);
                                }
                                if (cookie.indexOf(nameEq) === 0) {
                                    value = cookie.substring(nameEq.length, cookie.length);
                                }
                            });
                            return value;
                        }

                        window.guardian.config.ophan.browserId = getCookieValue("bwid");

                    })(window, document);
                </script>

class="dcr-5k6jfi" style="background-color:var(--masthead-nav-background);color:var(--masthead-nav-link-text)"><script>document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {

					/** The checkbox input element used to toggle the navigation menu. */
					const navInputCheckbox = document.getElementById('header-nav-input-checkbox');

					/** The veggie burger button element used to open/close the menu. */
					const veggieBurger = document.getElementById('header-veggie-burger');

					/** List of menu items that should be selectable when the menu is open. */
					const expandedMenuClickableTags = document.querySelectorAll(
						'.selectableMenuItem',
					);

					/** The root element of the expanded menu. */
					const expandedMenu = document.getElementById('header-expanded-menu-root');

					/** The label for the first column in the menu, assumed to be "News".*/
					const firstColLabel = document.getElementById('News-button');

					/** The link element in the second list item under news links. */
					const firstColLink = document.querySelector(
						'#newsLinks > li:nth-of-type(2) > a',
					);

					/**
					 * Focuses on the first navigation element depending on whether the first column label is visible.
					 *
					 * If the first column label is not visible, the function focuses on the first link element.
					 * Otherwise, it focuses on the first column label.
					 */
					const focusOnFirstNavElement = () => {
						if (window.getComputedStyle(firstColLabel).display === 'none') {
							firstColLink.focus();
						} else {
							firstColLabel.focus();
						}
					};

					/**
					 * Updates ARIA attributes and tabindex values based on whether the menu is open or closed.
					 */
					const updateAttributesForMenu = (isOpen) => {
						firstColLabel.setAttribute('aria-expanded', isOpen ? 'true' : 'false');
						veggieBurger.setAttribute(
							'data-link-name',
							isOpen
								? 'header : veggie-burger : hide'
								: 'header : veggie-burger : show',
						);
						expandedMenuClickableTags.forEach((tag) => {
							tag.setAttribute('tabindex', isOpen ? '0' : '-1');
						});
					};

					/** Toggles the navigation menu by simulating a click on the checkbox. */
					const toggleMainMenu = () => {
						if (navInputCheckbox) {
							navInputCheckbox.click();
						}
					};

					/**
					 * Handles keydown events to toggle the menu when the Enter or Space key is pressed.
					 */
					const keydownToggleMainMenu = (e) => {
						if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
							e.preventDefault();
							toggleMainMenu();
						}
					};
					/**
					 * Handles click events to manage the state of the navigation menu.
					 *
					 * - Toggles the menu open/close state when the menu button (veggieBurger) is clicked.
					 */
						const handleMenuClick = (e) => {
							const menuButtonClicked = navInputCheckbox === e.target;
							const clickInsideMenu = expandedMenu.contains(e.target);
							const menuIsOpen = navInputCheckbox.checked
							if (menuButtonClicked && !menuIsOpen) {
						    document.body.classList.toggle('nav-is-open')

							firstColLabel.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false')
                            veggieBurger.setAttribute('data-link-name','header : veggie-burger : show')
                            expandedMenuClickableTags.forEach(function($selectableElement){
                                $selectableElement.setAttribute('tabindex','-1')
                            })
                          } else if (menuButtonClicked && menuIsOpen) {
						    document.body.classList.toggle('nav-is-open')
							firstColLabel.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true')
                            veggieBurger.setAttribute('data-link-name','header : veggie-burger : hide')
                            expandedMenuClickableTags.forEach(function($selectableElement){
                                $selectableElement.setAttribute('tabindex','0')
                            })
                            focusOnFirstNavElement()
							}
						};

					/** Adds event listeners to manage the navigation menu. */
					if (navInputCheckbox) {
						navInputCheckbox.addEventListener('click', handleMenuClick);
						veggieBurger.addEventListener('keydown', keydownToggleMainMenu);
						document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
							if (e.key === 'Escape' && navInputCheckbox.checked) {
								toggleMainMenu();
								veggieBurger.focus();
							}
						});
					/**
					 * Handles mouse down events to manage the state of the navigation menu.
					 *
					 * - Closes the menu if the click occurs outside both the menu button and the expanded menu.
					 */
					document.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e){
						if(navInputCheckbox.checked && !expandedMenu.contains(e.target) && !veggieBurger.contains(e.target)){
						toggleMainMenu()
							}
						});
					}

within 30 days</h1><div class="dcr-1nvgr5i">This article is more than 7 years old</div></div></div></div><div class="dcr-1fnjjtg" data-gu-name="standfirst" style="--grid-area:standfirst"><div class="dcr-15in7js"><p>Federal ruling also prevents officials from splitting up families who crossed US-Mexico border illegally</p></div></div><aside class="dcr-1fnjjtg" data-gu-name="meta" style="--grid-area:meta"><div class="dcr-14emo0l"><div class="dcr-ich95x"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="dcr-194w08h" focusable="false" height="13" preserveaspectratio="none" stroke="var(--article-border)" stroke-width="1" viewbox="0 0 1300 13" width="100%" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><line x1="0" x2="1300" y1="0.5" y2="0.5"></line><line x1="0" x2="1300" y1="4.5" class="dcr-5oiine"><div class="dcr-1kpcv08"><div><address aria-label="Contributor info" data-component="meta-byline" data-gu-name="byline" data-link-name="byline"><div class="dcr-16bbvim"><a data-link-name="auto tag link" href="https://www.theguardian.com/profile/joannawalters" rel="author">Joanna Walters</a><span> in New York</span></div></address><details class="dcr-lp0nif" data-gu-name="dateline" style="--mobile-colour:var(--dateline)"><summary class="dcr-1ybxn6r"><span class="dcr-u0h1qy">Wed 27 Jun 2018 13.10 EDT</span></summary>First published on Wed 27 Jun 2018 00.35 EDT</details></div></div><div class="dcr-9dgpdq" data-print-layout="hide"><div class="dcr-16lnb0w"><gu-island deferuntil="visible" name="ShareButton" priority="feature" props='{"pageId":"us-news/2018/jun/27/us-immigration-must-reunite-families-separated-at-border-federal-judge-rules","webTitle":"Judge orders US to reunite families separated at border within 30 days","format":{"design":0,"display":0,"theme":0},"context":"ArticleMeta"}'><a class="dcr-125qj9d" href="mailto:?subject=Judge orders US to reunite families separated at border within 30 days&amp;body=https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2018/jun/27/us-immigration-must-reunite-families-separated-at-border-federal-judge-rules?CMP=share_btn_url" type="button">Share<div class="src-button-space"></div><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" viewbox="-3 -3 30 30" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path clip-rule="evenodd" d="M19 16c1.675 0 3 1.35 3 3 0 1.675-1.325 3-3 3a2.97 2.97 0 0 1-2.975-3c0-.125 0-.275.025-.375L7.1 14.15a2.9 2.9 0 0 1-2.075.825C3.325 14.975 2 13.65 2 12a3.004 3.004 0 0 1 3.025-3.025c.775 0 1.5.35 2.075.875l8.95-4.475c-.025-.1-.025-.225-.025-.4A2.966 2.966 0 0 1 19 2c1.675 0 3 1.325 3 2.975C22 6.65 20.675 8 19 8c-.8 0-1.475-.325-2.05-.825l-8.975 4.45C8 11.7 8 11.825 8 12s0 .3-.025.375l8.975 4.45c.575-.5 1.25-.825 2.05-.825m0-12.8c-.975 0-1.8.775-1.8 1.775S18.025 6.8 19 6.8c1 0 1.825-.825 1.825-1.825S20 3.2 19 3.2m0 17.6c1 0 1.825-.825 1.825-1.8 0-1-.825-1.8-1.825-1.8-.975 0-1.8.8-1.8 1.8 0 .975.825 1.8 1.8 1.8" fill-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></a></gu-island></div><div class="dcr-1csot3r"><div class="dcr-14baf59"><div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></aside><div class="dcr-st9szl" data-gu-name="body" style="--grid-area:body"><div class="dcr-1a4fred"><div class="dcr-1uvtuj9" id="maincontent"><div class="article-body-commercial-selector article-body-viewer-selector dcr-11jq3zt"><p class="dcr-130mj7b">A federal judge has ordered that <a data-component="auto-linked-tag" data-link-name="in body link" href="https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/usimmigration">US immigration</a> agents can no longer separate parents and children caught crossing the border from Mexico illegally and must work to reunite those families that have been split up within 30 days.</p><p class="dcr-130mj7b">Dana Sabraw, a district court judge in San Diego, granted the American Civil Liberties Union (ACLU) a preliminary injunction on Tuesday, which set a hard deadline in a process that until now had yielded uncertainty about when children might again see their parents.</p><div id="sign-in-gate"></div><p class="dcr-130mj7b">Children younger than five must be reunited with their families within 14 days, the court ruled.</p><p class="dcr-130mj7b">Tears will be flowing in detention centres across the country when the families learn they will be reunited, said Lee Gelernt, an ACLU lawyer, after the ruling.</p><p class="dcr-130mj7b">It is not clear how border authorities will meet the deadline, however. The health and human services secretary, Alex Azar, told Congress on Tuesday that his department still had custody of 2,047 children separated from their parents at the border. That is only six fewer than the number in HHS custody last Wednesday. Democratic senators said that was not nearly enough progress.</p><p class="dcr-130mj7b">Sabraw, an appointee of former president George W Bush, issued a nationwide injunction on future family separations, except where the parent is deemed unfit or does not want to be with the child. His ruling requires that the government provide phone contact between parents and their children within 10 days.</p><p class="dcr-130mj7b">Following national and international outcry, <a data-component="auto-linked-tag" data-link-name="in body link" href="https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/donaldtrump">Donald Trump</a> signed an executive order last week mandating that families entering the US illegally would no longer be separated under his administrations zero-tolerance immigration policy.</p><p class="dcr-130mj7b">Before the preliminary injunction ruling, the government urged Sabraw not to rule that it must stop separating families and quickly reunite them, saying Trumps executive order last week largely addressed those goals.<strong> <br/></strong></p><p class="dcr-130mj7b">But the judge disagreed. The facts set forth before the court portray reactive governance responses to address a chaotic circumstance of the governments own making, Sabraw wrote. They belie measured and ordered governance, which is central to the concept of due process enshrined in our constitution.</p><p class="dcr-130mj7b">Tuesdays ruling  which came after the supreme court <a data-link-name="in body link" href="https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2018/jun/26/trump-supreme-court-upholds-travel-ban">upheld Trumps travel ban</a> targeting five Muslim-majority countries  could open up a legal battle with the justice department, which has blamed elected politicians in Congress for the mess.</p><p class="dcr-130mj7b">The DoJ said the ruling makes it even more imperative for Congress to pass immigration legislation that would enable the government to simultaneously enforce the law and keep families together.</p><p class="dcr-130mj7b">Without this action by Congress, lawlessness at the border will continue, the department said.</p><p class="dcr-130mj7b">Congress is braced for a vote later on Wednesday on an immigration bill that is designed as a compromise between moderate and conservative factions of the congressional Republicans. It is on track for defeat.</p><p class="dcr-130mj7b">The bill would provide $25bn in US taxpayers money for a wall on the Mexican border, even though Trump pledged repeatedly during the 2016 election campaign that he would force Mexico to pay for it.</p><p class="dcr-130mj7b">It would also limit legal immigration; provide a pathway to citizenship for eligible young undocumented immigrants, known as Dreamers; and officially ban family separations at the border. But Democrats and hardline conservative Republicans are refusing to support it.</p><p class="dcr-130mj7b">In the face of defeat, some Republicans were considering a plan B: passing narrower legislation by the end of the week curbing the Trump administrations contentious separating of migrant families.</p><p class="dcr-130mj7b">Simon Sandoval-Moshenberg, of the Legal Aid Justice Centre in Virginia, said attorneys had spoken to about 200 immigrants at the Port Isabel detention facility near Los Fresnos, Texas, since last week, and only a few knew where their children were being held.</p><p class="dcr-130mj7b">The US government never had any plan to reunite these families that were separated, he said, and it was now scrambling to undo this terrible thing that they have done.</p><figure class="dcr-47fhrn" data-spacefinder-role="richLink" data-spacefinder-type="model.dotcomrendering.pageElements.RichLinkBlockElement" class="dcr-130mj7b">On Tuesday, 17 states including New York and California sued the Trump administration to try to force it to reunite children and parents. The states, all of which have Democratic attorneys general, joined Washington DC in filing the lawsuit in a federal court in Seattle, arguing that they were being forced to shoulder increased child welfare, education and social services costs.<br/></p><p class="dcr-130mj7b">In a speech before the conservative Criminal Justice Legal Foundation in Los Angeles, the US attorney general, Jeff Sessions, defended the administration for taking a hardline stand on illegal immigration and said voters had elected Trump to do just that.<br/></p><p class="dcr-130mj7b">This is the Trump era, he said. We are enforcing our laws again. We know whose side we are on  and were on the side of police and were on the side of the public safety of the American people. <br/></p><p class="dcr-130mj7b">Many people outraged by the family separations have staged protests in recent days in states including Florida and Texas. In Los Angeles, police arrested 25 demonstrators at a rally on Tuesday before Sessions gave his address.</p><p class="dcr-130mj7b">Outside Sessions office, protesters carried signs reading Free the children! and Stop caging families. Clergy members who blocked the street by forming a human chain were handcuffed by police and led away.</p></div></div><gu-island deferuntil="visible" name="SlotBodyEnd" priority="feature"
